(Ios)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 583)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 583).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 20).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 214).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 615)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 615).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 475).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 198).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 409)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 409).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 930).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 404).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 773)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 773).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 1678).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 37).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 727)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 727).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 2133).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 44).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 553)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 553).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 2588).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 250).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 576)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.08).cgColor

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 584)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 584).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 475).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 1389).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 399)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 399).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 930).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 1625).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 696)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 696).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 2133).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 1328).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 553)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 40)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.2).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 20
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 40
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 553).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 2588).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 1471).isActive = true

var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)

layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 364, height: 534)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 364).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 534).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 716).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 154).isActive = true

var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 364, height: 576)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 364).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 576).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 1796).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 106).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 364, height: 662)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 364).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 662).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 2249).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 20).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 364, height: 466)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 364).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 466).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 3053).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 178).isActive = true

var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 364, height: 508)
var shadows = UIView()
shadows.frame = view.frame
shadows.clipsToBounds = false
view.addSubview(shadows)


let shadowPath0 = UIBezierPath(roundedRect: shadows.bounds, cornerRadius: 36)
let layer0 = CALayer()
layer0.shadowPath = shadowPath0.cgPath
layer0.shadowColor = UIColor(red: 0.647, green: 0.647, blue: 0.647, alpha: 0.08).cgColor
layer0.shadowOpacity = 1
layer0.shadowRadius = 8
layer0.shadowOffset = CGSize(width: 0, height: 2)
layer0.bounds = shadows.bounds
layer0.position = shadows.center
shadows.layer.addSublayer(layer0)


var shapes = UIView()
shapes.frame = view.frame
shapes.clipsToBounds = true
view.addSubview(shapes)


let layer1 = CALayer()
layer1.backgroundColor = UIColor(red: 0.988, green: 0.988, blue: 0.988, alpha: 1).cgColor
layer1.bounds = shapes.bounds
layer1.position = shapes.center
shapes.layer.addSublayer(layer1)


shapes.layer.cornerRadius = 36
shapes.layer.borderWidth = 1
shapes.layer.borderColor = UIColor(red: 0.067, green: 0.067, blue: 0.067, alpha: 0.1).cgColor


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 364).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 508).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 3544).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 176).isActive = true

(iOS)
var view = UIView()
view.frame = CGRect(x: 0, y: 0, width: 393, height: 788)


var parent = self.view!
parent.addSubview(view)
view.translatesAutoresizingMaskIntoConstraints = false
view.widthAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 393).isActive = true
view.heightAnchor.constraint(equalToConstant: 788).isActive = true
view.leadingAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.leadingAnchor, constant: 468).isActive = true
view.topAnchor.constraint(equalTo: parent.topAnchor, constant: 20).isActive = true
